2. (būvis) readiness, preparedness

pasisakymas /paʂirʲˈɪnʲktʲi/ <n, m>
1. utterance, (pareiškimas) statement, pronouncement
2. (kalba) speech, speaking
3. (prisipažinimas) confession
pasisakyti /paʂirʲiːʑˈɪmas/ <v>
1. (tarti žodį) speak (out), (savo nuomonę) express/ state one's opinion, have/say one's say, (kokiu klausimu) speak on the question (of)
2. (už, prieš) speak (for, against), declare (for against), come out (for, against)
3. (prisipažinti) confess
4. (apie save) tell of oneself
